The|O proposed|O method|O to|O perform|O integrated|O analysis|O of|O functional|O and|O structural|O connectivity|O is|O illustrated|O in|O Fig|O 1|O .|O

Cortical|O reconstruction|O and|O volumetric|O segmentation|O of|O each|O subject|O ’|O s|O T1|O image|O to|O produce|O an|O ROI|O atlas|O was|O performed|O using|O the|O FreeSurfer|B-Application_Usage image|O analysis|O suite|O [17]|O ,|O available|O online|O at|O http://surfer.nmr.mgh.harvard.edu|O .|O
The|O atlas|O was|O registered|O with|O 12|O degrees|O of|O freedom|O to|O both|O the|O DWI|O ’|O s|O b0|O image|O and|O a|O mean|O fMRI|O ,|O also|O using|O FSL|B-Application_Usage ’|O s|O FLIRT|B-PlugIn_Usage algorithm|O .|O
The|O DWI|O '|O s|O were|O preprocessed|O using|O AFNI|B-Application_Usage and|O FSL|B-Application_Usage tools|O [18]|O .|O
First|O they|O were|O corrected|O for|O motion|O and|O Eddy|O currents|O and|O the|O brain|O extraction|O tool|O was|O used|O for|O skull|O stripping|O of|O the|O Eddy|O -|O corrected|O DWI|O .|O

FA|O and|O mean|O diffusivity|O (|O MD|O )|O images|O were|O generated|O from|O the|O skull|O -|O stripped|O DWI|O using|O DTIFit|B-PlugIn_Usage .|O
All|O three|O images|O (|O DWI|O ,|O FA|O and|O MD|O )|O were|O masked|O using|O a|O mask|O generated|O from|O the|O registered|O FreeSurfer|B-Application_Usage image|O ,|O including|O cortex|O ,|O white|O matter|O and|O subcortical|O regions|O .|O
The|O network|O extraction|O step|O of|O the|O “|O Statistical|B-Application_Usage Analysis|I-Application_Usage of|I-Application_Usage Minimum|I-Application_Usage cost|I-Application_Usage path|I-Application_Usage based|I-Application_Usage Structural|I-Application_Usage Connectivity|I-Application_Usage ”|O (|O SAMSCo|O )|O framework|O [4]|O was|O used|O to|O define|O structural|O connectivity|O because|O it|O minimizes|O the|O influence|O of|O directional|O uncertainty|O while|O finding|O globally|O optimal|O paths|O .|O
A|O minimum|O cost|O path|O network|O (|O DMC|O )|O was|O extracted|O ,|O with|O nodes|O defined|O by|O ROIs|O in|O the|O registered|O atlas|O and|O edges|O defined|O as|O minimum|O cumulative|O cost|O to|O travel|O between|O ROIs|O .|O
A|O second|O metric|O of|O structural|O connectivity|O ,|O the|O average|O fractional|O anisotropy|O (|O DFA|O )|O network|O ,|O was|O produced|O by|O dividing|O the|O sum|O of|O fractional|O anisotropy|O along|O a|O minimum|O cost|O path|O by|O the|O Euclidean|O distance|O of|O the|O path|O .|O
SAMSCo|B-Application_Mention produces|O two|O values|O per|O connection|O ,|O one|O from|O the|O seed|O to|O target|O region|O and|O the|O other|O from|O the|O target|O to|O seed|O region|O .|O
Therefore|O ,|O the|O SAMSCo|B-Application_Usage networks|O were|O symmetrized|O by|O choosing|O the|O minimum|O of|O the|O two|O costs|O (|O and|O corresponding|O DFA|O values|O )|O to|O represent|O the|O edge|O between|O each|O pair|O of|O regions|O .|O
It|O is|O important|O to|O note|O that|O SAMSCo|B-Application_Mention is|O a|O less|O traditional|O choice|O of|O structural|O connectivity|O measure|O ,|O an|O aspect|O which|O is|O discussed|O in|O more|O detail|O in|O the|O “|O Image|O preprocessing|O and|O network|O generation|O ”|O subsection|O of|O the|O Discussion|O section|O .|O
Preprocessing|O of|O the|O fMRI|O '|O s|O was|O accomplished|O using|O ANFI|B-Application_Usage and|O FSL|B-Application_Usage tools|O [18,19]|O .|O
The|O fMRI|O images|O were|O slice|O -|O timing|O and|O motion|O -|O corrected|O ,|O both|O using|O AFNI|B-Application_Usage tools|O .|O
The|O first|O four|O TRs|O were|O removed|O to|O allow|O for|O equilibration|O and|O a|O temporal|O 0.01Hz|O high|O pass|O filter|O was|O applied|O to|O remove|O low|O frequency|O signals|O .|O
Global|O mean|O ,|O mean|O cerebral|O spinal|O fluid|O ,|O and|O mean|O white|O matter|O time|O series|O as|O well|O as|O the|O six|O motion|O parameters|O resulting|O from|O motion|O correction|O were|O regressed|O out|O from|O the|O image|O .|O
Finally|O ,|O an|O 8mm|O full|O -|O width|O -|O half|O -|O maximum|O Gaussian|O spatial|O filter|O [20]|O was|O applied|O to|O increase|O the|O signal|O to|O noise|O ratio|O .|O
We|O defined|O two|O atlas|O -|O based|O metrics|O for|O defining|O functional|O connectivity|O .|O
Typically|O ,|O functional|O connectivity|O studies|O include|O a|O preprocessing|O step|O where|O fMRI|O images|O are|O spatially|O normalized|O to|O a|O common|O reference|O space|O and|O blurred|O to|O account|O for|O differences|O in|O structural|O and|O functional|O variability|O .|O
However|O ,|O anatomical|O and|O functional|O variation|O between|O subjects|O can|O be|O large|O [20]|O ,|O and|O thus|O the|O deformations|O involved|O in|O spatial|O normalization|O may|O stretch|O or|O contract|O parts|O of|O the|O brain|O for|O some|O subjects|O more|O than|O others|O .|O
In|O this|O study|O ,|O spatial|O normalization|O was|O not|O performed|O .|O

This|O reduced|O the|O effects|O of|O structural|O variability|O .|O
The|O average|O time|O series|O for|O each|O ROI|O was|O calculated|O .|O

Integrated|O analysis|O and|O visualization|O of|O structural|O and|O functional|O networks|O :|O An|O ordinary|O least|O squares|O linear|O regression|O model|O was|O estimated|O for|O each|O connection|O including|O group|O membership|O ,|O modeled|O as|O a|O single|O variable|O containing|O zeros|O and|O ones|O ,|O and|O covariates|O as|O variables|O ,|O along|O with|O a|O constant|O term|O to|O model|O the|O mean|O of|O the|O data|O .|O

This|O reordering|O gives|O an|O indication|O of|O the|O distribution|O of|O points|O within|O each|O cluster|O ,|O and|O enables|O simultaneous|O plotting|O and|O comparison|O of|O multiple|O network|O measures|O .|O

We|O instead|O used|O −|O log|O 10|O (|O p|O )|O *|O sign|O (|O t|O )|O *|O s0|O .05|O ,|O Meff|O ,|O G|O ,|O where|O t|O is|O the|O t|O -|O statistic|O of|O a|O given|O connection|O ,|O p|O is|O the|O corresponding|O p|O -|O value|O and|O s|O α|O ,|O Meff|O ,|O G|O =|O log|O 10|O (|O α|O )|O /|O log|O 10|O (|O α|O Meff|O ,|O G|O )|O is|O a|O scaling|O factor|O used|O to|O ensure|O that|O the|O reference|O line|O corresponding|O to|O the|O adjusted|O significance|O threshold|O ,|O α|O Meff|O ,|O G|O (|O see|O below|O for|O details|O of|O its|O derivation|O )|O ,|O is|O the|O same|O for|O all|O networks|O G|O .|O sign|O (|O t|O )|O adds|O information|O about|O whether|O an|O observed|O association|O is|O positive|O or|O negative|O .|O

When|O the|O eye|O was|O fixated|O on|O the|O fixation|O point|O (|O online|O ,|O measured|O by|O eye|O tracker|O ,|O and|O the|O deviance|O was|O less|O than|O 0.5|O °|O )|O ,|O another|O dim|O dot|O (|O diameter|O :|O 0.17|O °|O ;|O luminance|O :|O 0.028|O cd|O /|O m2|O )|O appeared|O .|O

The|O participant|O had|O to|O indicate|O if|O the|O moving|O dot|O vanished|O to|O the|O right|O or|O to|O the|O left|O of|O the|O reference|O lines|O ,|O which|O were|O positioned|O randomly|O between|O 0|O °|O and|O 1.8|O °|O with|O a|O step|O size|O of|O 0.3|O °|O away|O from|O the|O fixation|O point|O (|O on|O the|O same|O side|O as|O the|O movement|O )|O .|O

The|O task|O was|O to|O indicate|O if|O the|O moving|O dot|O '|O s|O first|O perceived|O position|O was|O to|O the|O left|O or|O the|O right|O of|O the|O reference|O lines|O .|O

In|O Experiment|O 2|O ,|O the|O stimuli|O and|O procedure|O were|O the|O same|O as|O in|O Experiment|O 1|O ,|O excepting|O the|O following|O differences|O :|O A|O blue|O (|O Tokyo|O blue|O LEE|O filter|O ,|O dominant|O wave|O length|O :|O 422|O nm|O )|O or|O a|O green|O (|O Primary|O green|O LEE|O filter|O ,|O dominant|O wave|O length|O :|O 501|O nm|O )|O plastic|O filter|O was|O attached|O on|O the|O surface|O of|O the|O monitor|O in|O separated|O sessions|O .|O
We|O used|O the|O cyan|O color|O for|O all|O stimuli|O on|O the|O screen|O to|O reduce|O the|O red|O spectrum|O .|O

Participants|O '|O responses|O were|O first|O converted|O to|O proportions|O of|O visibility|O for|O the|O detection|O task|O ,|O the|O motion|O -|O initiated|O and|O motion|O -|O terminated|O localization|O tasks|O .|O
Psychometric|O curves|O were|O then|O fitted|O using|O a|O logistic|O function|O to|O each|O condition|O and|O points|O of|O subjective|O equality|O (|O PSEs|O )|O were|O estimated|O from|O the|O 50|O %|O point|O of|O corresponding|O psychometric|O function|O .|O
Although|O it|O is|O common|O to|O observe|O occlusions|O for|O multi|O -|O object|O motion|O in|O single|O -|O view|O images|O ,|O objects|O may|O actually|O be|O physically|O distant|O from|O each|O other|O and|O an|O occlusion|O may|O not|O exist|O at|O all|O if|O the|O observation|O is|O made|O in|O 3D|O space|O .|O
In|O fact|O ,|O an|O occlusion|O is|O caused|O by|O different|O observation|O perspectives|O .|O
Therefore|O ,|O in|O order|O to|O solve|O occlusions|O in|O the|O tracking|O process|O ,|O three|O cameras|O are|O used|O to|O capture|O objects|O ’|O motion|O from|O different|O directions|O simultaneously|O (|O Fig|O 1|O )|O .|O
Thus|O ,|O integrated|O multi|O -|O view|O tracking|O results|O are|O able|O to|O accurately|O acquire|O 3D|O motion|O trajectories|O .|O
The|O proposed|O method|O is|O introduced|O in|O two|O parts|O ,|O object|O detection|O and|O object|O tracking|O ,|O respectively|O .|O

Three|O synchronized|O cameras|O capture|O swimming|O behavior|O from|O one|O top|O -|O view|O and|O two|O side|O -|O view|O directions|O .|O
Each|O pair|O of|O the|O three|O directions|O are|O vertical|O to|O one|O another|O .|O
All|O experimental|O procedures|O were|O in|O compliance|O with|O the|O Institutional|O Animal|O Care|O and|O Use|O Committee|O (|O IACUC|O )|O of|O Shanghai|O Research|O Center|O for|O Model|O Organisms|O (|O Shanghai|O ,|O China|O )|O with|O approval|O ID|O 2010|O -|O 0010|O ,|O and|O all|O efforts|O were|O made|O to|O minimize|O suffering|O .|O
This|O study|O was|O approved|O by|O the|O Institutional|O Animal|O Care|O and|O Use|O Committee|O (|O IACUC|O )|O ,|O and|O written|O informed|O consent|O was|O obtained|O .|O
In|O the|O laboratory|O environment|O ,|O objects|O move|O in|O a|O stationary|O container|O so|O the|O background|O is|O relatively|O stable|O .|O
Therefore|O ,|O motion|O regions|O can|O be|O segmented|O effectively|O with|O the|O aid|O of|O a|O background|O subtraction|O method|O :|O Rt|O (|O x|O ,|O y|O )|O =|O {|O 1|O ,|O formtok|O where|O fb|O (|O x|O ,|O y|O )|O represents|O the|O background|O obtained|O by|O calculating|O the|O average|O of|O N|O consecutive|O frames|O of|O video|O sequences|O .|O
Since|O rough|O edges|O in|O the|O motion|O region|O are|O not|O conducive|O for|O the|O extraction|O and|O analysis|O of|O the|O main|O skeleton|O ,|O some|O preprocessing|O is|O necessary|O .|O
Isolated|O interior|O pixels|O of|O the|O moving|O region|O are|O first|O filled|O ,|O and|O small|O interfering|O blocks|O are|O then|O removed|O .|O
Finally|O ,|O a|O median|O filter|O is|O used|O to|O smooth|O the|O boundary|O .|O
Fig|O 2|O shows|O the|O effects|O of|O preprocessing|O on|O the|O motion|O regions|O .|O
Preprocessing|O is|O shown|O to|O effectively|O reduce|O detail|O interferences|O while|O preserving|O the|O main|O structure|O of|O the|O motion|O regions|O .|O
Figure|O data|O removed|O from|O full|O text|O .|O
Figure|O identifier|O and|O caption|O :|O 10.1371/journal.pone.0180254.g002|O The|O main|O skeleton|O obtained|O using|O different|O thresholds|O Tu|O .|O
With|O an|O increase|O in|O the|O value|O of|O threshold|O Tu|O ,|O the|O obtained|O skeleton|O can|O better|O represent|O the|O main|O structure|O of|O the|O motion|O region|O while|O ignoring|O more|O details|O .|O (|O a|O )|O Top|O view|O .|O (|O b|O )|O Side|O view|O .|O
Since|O the|O object|O has|O a|O belt|O -|O like|O appearance|O ,|O its|O center|O curve|O can|O be|O obtained|O through|O extraction|O of|O the|O main|O skeleton|O ,|O thus|O transforming|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O structure|O from|O a|O 2D|O region|O to|O a|O 1D|O curve|O .|O
It|O also|O alleviates|O tracking|O difficulty|O by|O reducing|O the|O number|O of|O pixel|O points|O that|O need|O to|O be|O tracked|O .|O
In|O the|O existing|O skeleton|O extraction|O methods|O ,|O the|O augmented|O fast|O marching|O method|O (|O AFMM|O )|O [19]|O is|O used|O to|O extract|O the|O main|O skeleton|O .|O
First|O ,|O an|O arrival|O time|O U|O is|O set|O for|O each|O point|O at|O the|O edge|O of|O the|O region|O .|O
Then|O ,|O the|O value|O of|O U|O for|O the|O entire|O region|O is|O obtained|O by|O iteration|O of|O the|O fast|O marching|O method|O .|O
Based|O on|O the|O distribution|O of|O U|O ,|O skeleton|O points|O can|O be|O defined|O as|O :|O formtok|O s.t|O .|O formtok|O which|O show|O that|O a|O given|O point|O (|O i|O ,|O j|O )|O is|O regarded|O as|O a|O skeleton|O point|O when|O the|O difference|O of|O U|O between|O this|O point|O and|O its|O neighbors|O in|O the|O x|O and|O y|O directions|O is|O larger|O than|O the|O threshold|O Tu|O .|O
The|O reasons|O for|O choosing|O AFMM|O are|O as|O follows|O :|O
(|O 1|O )|O Speed|O of|O operation|O .|O
Considering|O that|O each|O frame|O contains|O many|O motion|O regions|O ,|O a|O low|O skeleton|O extraction|O efficiency|O has|O a|O significant|O influence|O on|O tracking|O performance|O .|O
As|O one|O of|O the|O fastest|O skeleton|O extraction|O methods|O ,|O AFMM|O is|O particularly|O suitable|O for|O skeleton|O extraction|O of|O regions|O in|O video|O images|O .|O
(|O 2|O )|O Multi|O -|O scale|O skeleton|O representation|O .|O
Although|O preprocessing|O is|O ,|O to|O some|O extent|O ,|O conducive|O to|O extraction|O of|O the|O main|O skeleton|O ,|O it|O cannot|O completely|O remove|O interference|O of|O small|O branches|O .|O
A|O simple|O and|O effective|O way|O to|O accurately|O extract|O the|O main|O skeleton|O of|O motion|O regions|O is|O to|O analyze|O the|O region|O for|O different|O scales|O in|O order|O to|O find|O an|O optimal|O scale|O for|O skeleton|O extraction|O .|O
The|O function|O of|O the|O threshold|O Tu|O in|O AFMM|O is|O similar|O to|O a|O scale|O factor|O .|O
A|O smaller|O threshold|O provides|O more|O skeleton|O details|O ,|O and|O a|O large|O threshold|O provides|O less|O skeleton|O details|O .|O
Fig|O 2|O shows|O skeleton|O extraction|O results|O for|O different|O threshold|O values|O .|O
Results|O demonstrate|O that|O ,|O as|O the|O threshold|O Tu|O increases|O ,|O skeleton|O details|O gradually|O decrease|O ,|O but|O the|O skeleton|O '|O s|O ability|O to|O describe|O the|O main|O structure|O of|O the|O object|O gradually|O increases|O .|O
After|O obtaining|O the|O main|O skeleton|O ,|O points|O that|O best|O represent|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O shape|O are|O selected|O as|O feature|O points|O ,|O which|O further|O simplifies|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O structure|O .|O
First|O ,|O a|O point|O in|O the|O main|O skeleton|O is|O selected|O to|O represent|O the|O center|O position|O of|O the|O object|O .|O
In|O the|O skeleton|O obtained|O through|O AFMM|O ,|O the|O maximum|O U|O value|O is|O usually|O located|O at|O the|O center|O ,|O which|O better|O reflects|O the|O midpoint|O of|O the|O motion|O region|O .|O
Therefore|O ,|O this|O point|O is|O defined|O as|O the|O central|O feature|O point|O of|O the|O object|O .|O
Compared|O with|O the|O centroid|O of|O the|O motion|O region|O ,|O the|O maximum|O U|O point|O has|O better|O stability|O since|O it|O is|O less|O susceptible|O to|O changes|O in|O the|O shape|O of|O the|O motion|O region|O .|O
Then|O ,|O by|O considering|O the|O discrepancy|O in|O objects|O ’|O appearances|O from|O different|O views|O ,|O two|O feature|O point|O models|O are|O used|O to|O represent|O the|O objects|O in|O the|O top|O view|O and|O side|O view|O ,|O respectively|O .|O
As|O shown|O in|O Fig|O 3|O (|O a|O )|O ,|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O appearance|O in|O the|O top|O view|O has|O the|O following|O characteristics|O :|O
(|O 1|O )|O It|O is|O composed|O of|O two|O parts|O ,|O the|O rigid|O first|O -|O half|O region|O that|O has|O less|O deformation|O ,|O and|O the|O non|O -|O rigid|O second|O -|O half|O region|O that|O has|O greater|O deformation|O ;|O and|O (|O 2|O )|O The|O structure|O gradually|O becomes|O narrower|O from|O head|O to|O the|O tail|O .|O
Based|O on|O the|O above|O characteristics|O ,|O two|O points|O can|O be|O selected|O from|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O main|O skeleton|O as|O its|O head|O and|O tail|O .|O
First|O ,|O the|O average|O width|O of|O skeleton|O points|O on|O both|O sides|O of|O the|O central|O feature|O point|O are|O obtained|O using|O the|O shortest|O distance|O between|O the|O skeleton|O point|O and|O the|O region|O edge|O as|O the|O radius|O .|O
Then|O ,|O the|O corresponding|O skeleton|O of|O the|O rigid|O region|O can|O be|O distinguished|O from|O that|O of|O the|O non|O -|O rigid|O region|O based|O on|O the|O average|O width|O .|O
Since|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O main|O skeleton|O has|O endpoints|O at|O the|O head|O and|O tail|O positions|O ,|O skeleton|O endpoints|O of|O the|O object|O '|O s|O rigid|O and|O non|O -|O rigid|O regions|O are|O defined|O as|O the|O head|O feature|O point|O and|O tail|O feature|O point|O .|O
Then|O ,|O a|O double|O feature|O point|O model|O (|O DFPM|O )|O comprised|O of|O the|O head|O feature|O point|O and|O central|O feature|O point|O is|O used|O to|O represent|O the|O object|O as|O shown|O in|O Fig|O 3|O (|O b|O )|O .|O
DFPM|O has|O the|O following|O advantages|O :|O
(|O 1|O )|O Simple|O and|O accurate|O .|O
It|O is|O composed|O of|O two|O points|O of|O the|O rigid|O region|O of|O the|O object|O ,|O and|O can|O accurately|O reflect|O the|O object|O '|O s|O spatial|O location|O ;|O and|O (|O 2|O )|O Comprehensive|O information|O .|O
It|O not|O only|O indicates|O the|O object|O ’|O s|O location|O ,|O but|O denotes|O the|O motion|O direction|O ,|O thus|O reducing|O the|O difficulty|O in|O object|O tracking|O .|O

The|O blue|O line|O represents|O the|O main|O skeleton|O of|O fish|O .|O

By|O means|O of|O equation|O (|O 1|O )|O ,|O the|O capacity|O dimension|O is|O estimated|O as|O D0|O =|O 1|O /|O d|O ≈|O 0.878|O ,|O and|O the|O goodness|O of|O fit|O is|O about|O R|O 2|O =|O 0.990|O ;|O By|O means|O of|O equation|O (|O 24|O )|O and|O (|O 25|O )|O ,|O the|O correlation|O dimension|O is|O estimated|O as|O D2|O ≈|O 1.296|O ,|O and|O the|O goodness|O of|O fit|O is|O around|O R|O 2|O =|O 0.977|O .|O
This|O implies|O D0|O <|O D2|O ,|O and|O the|O result|O is|O abnormal|O .|O
However|O ,|O if|O we|O replace|O the|O least|O square|O method|O with|O the|O nonlinear|O fit|O method|O ,|O the|O results|O are|O D0|O ≈|O 1.225|O ,|O D2|O ≈|O 1.012|O ,|O respectively|O .|O
This|O time|O ,|O D0|O >|O D2|O ,|O and|O this|O seems|O to|O be|O normal|O .|O
As|O is|O often|O the|O case|O ,|O different|O algorithms|O yield|O different|O results|O and|O then|O lead|O to|O different|O conclusions|O .|O

The|O least|O square|O method|O benefits|O the|O medium|O -|O sized|O cities|O and|O small|O cities|O (|O Figure|O 2|O )|O ,|O while|O the|O nonlinear|O fit|O method|O favors|O large|O cities|O .|O
In|O fact|O ,|O the|O rank|O -|O size|O distribution|O can|O be|O transformed|O into|O a|O self|O -|O similar|O hierarchy|O ,|O and|O then|O we|O can|O estimate|O the|O fractal|O dimension|O of|O the|O city|O -|O size|O distribution|O with|O the|O generalized|O 2n|O rule|O [17]|O ,|O [38]|O .|O
By|O the|O 2n|O principle|O ,|O the|O capacity|O dimension|O is|O estimated|O as|O D0|O ≈|O 0.992|O (|O d0|O ≈|O 1.008|O )|O ,|O and|O R|O 2|O =|O 0.990|O .|O
In|O this|O instance|O ,|O the|O correlation|O dimension|O is|O expected|O to|O approach|O 1|O ,|O that|O is|O ,|O formtok|O (|O Table|O 3|O )|O .|O
The|O self|O -|O similar|O hierarchy|O can|O filter|O the|O random|O disturbance|O of|O various|O noises|O so|O that|O the|O result|O is|O more|O stable|O and|O dependable|O .|O
It|O can|O be|O seen|O that|O the|O size|O sequence|O of|O cities|O in|O the|O real|O world|O is|O more|O complicated|O than|O the|O p|O -|O sequence|O in|O the|O mathematical|O world|O .|O

Table|O identifier|O and|O caption|O :|O 10.1371/journal.pone.0024791.t003|O Different|O approaches|O to|O estimating|O the|O fractal|O dimension|O values|O of|O the|O U.S|O .|O city|O -|O size|O distribution|O (|O 2000|O )|O .|O
Applying|O the|O hierarchical|O correlational|O analysis|O to|O the|O U.S|O .|O cities|O gives|O us|O an|O insight|O into|O the|O city|O -|O size|O distributions|O .|O
For|O the|O 513|O top|O U.S|O .|O cities|O ,|O the|O data|O points|O actually|O follow|O along|O two|O trend|O lines|O with|O different|O slopes|O .|O
The|O large|O cities|O in|O the|O minority|O (|O about|O 32|O cities|O )|O share|O one|O trend|O line|O (|O the|O slope|O is|O d0|O ≈|O 0.763|O ,|O thus|O D0|O ≈|O 1.311|O )|O ,|O while|O the|O medium|O -|O sized|O and|O small|O cities|O (|O about|O 481|O cities|O )|O in|O the|O majority|O share|O another|O one|O (|O the|O slope|O is|O d0|O ≈|O 1.235|O ,|O thus|O D0|O ≈|O 0.810|O )|O .|O
This|O suggests|O that|O the|O large|O U.S|O .|O cities|O took|O on|O Zipf|O '|O s|O effect|O ,|O but|O the|O medium|O and|O small|O cities|O presented|O the|O Pareto|O effect|O .|O
The|O large|O cities|O tried|O to|O become|O larger|O ,|O while|O the|O medium|O and|O small|O cities|O tried|O to|O become|O more|O than|O ever|O .|O
However|O ,|O where|O statistical|O average|O is|O concerned|O ,|O the|O two|O effects|O seem|O to|O be|O balanced|O .|O
In|O theory|O ,|O in|O order|O to|O reconcile|O the|O two|O effects|O of|O city|O development|O ,|O the|O scaling|O exponents|O (|O d0|O ,|O D0|O )|O approach|O 1|O in|O the|O process|O of|O urbanization|O .|O
But|O for|O the|O real|O cities|O ,|O the|O competition|O of|O the|O two|O effects|O often|O breaks|O the|O scaling|O relation|O so|O that|O one|O tread|O line|O divides|O into|O two|O on|O log|O -|O log|O plots|O .|O
The|O cause|O of|O the|O scaling|O breaking|O may|O be|O as|O follows|O .|O
People|O attach|O more|O importance|O to|O and|O invest|O heavily|O in|O large|O cities|O ,|O but|O the|O geographical|O space|O and|O natural|O environment|O cannot|O support|O the|O grand|O -|O scale|O population|O of|O a|O city|O .|O
On|O the|O other|O ,|O people|O pay|O less|O attention|O to|O and|O invest|O lightly|O to|O smaller|O cities|O ,|O which|O are|O usually|O undergrown|O .|O
The|O result|O is|O that|O both|O the|O largest|O cities|O and|O smallest|O cities|O fail|O to|O reach|O the|O sizes|O predicted|O by|O the|O pure|O form|O of|O Zipf|O '|O s|O law|O (|O d|O =|O 1|O )|O .|O
In|O fact|O ,|O the|O correlational|O model|O can|O also|O be|O applied|O to|O the|O cities|O in|O the|O developing|O countries|O such|O as|O China|O and|O India|O (|O see|O Text|O S3|O )|O .|O

The|O damselfish|O Pomacentrus|O amboinensis|O is|O common|O on|O coral|O reefs|O of|O the|O Indo|O -|O Pacific|O .|O
Males|O and|O females|O are|O strongly|O site|O attached|O and|O often|O live|O in|O a|O discrete|O group|O .|O
P|O .|O amboinensis|O has|O a|O pelagic|O larval|O duration|O of|O 15|O -|O 23|O days|O and|O settles|O at|O 10.3|O -|O 15.1|O mm|O standard|O length|O with|O its|O juvenile|O body|O plan|O largely|O complete|O [33]|O .|O
Although|O P|O .|O amboinensis|O settle|O to|O a|O wide|O variety|O of|O habitats|O on|O reefs|O of|O the|O northern|O Great|O Barrier|O Reef|O they|O are|O found|O in|O highest|O densities|O associated|O with|O mixed|O live|O coral|O ,|O rubble|O and|O sand|O areas|O on|O the|O shallow|O reef|O base|O or|O reef|O slope|O .|O
A|O tagging|O study|O of|O 295|O newly|O settled|O fish|O on|O the|O continuous|O reef|O edge|O found|O that|O fish|O moved|O little|O over|O the|O first|O 3|O months|O after|O settlement|O (|O mean|O =|O 0.63|O m|O [34]|O )|O .|O
A|O recent|O study|O showed|O that|O P|O .|O amboinensis|O who|O had|O newly|O metamorphosed|O in|O light|O traps|O displayed|O a|O dramatic|O and|O statistically|O significant|O preference|O for|O live|O coral|O (|O Pocillopora|O damicornis|O )|O over|O bleached|O ,|O dead|O coral|O or|O sand|O habitats|O in|O selection|O trials|O conducted|O in|O 500|O l|O circular|O tanks|O [35]|O .|O
Studies|O of|O this|O species|O also|O suggest|O high|O levels|O of|O mortality|O are|O typical|O within|O the|O first|O 24|O h|O on|O the|O reef|O ,|O with|O values|O of|O up|O to|O 98|O %|O mortality|O being|O recorded|O (|O mean|O ∼|O 50|O %|O )|O [9]|O ,|O [10]|O .|O
Interestingly|O ,|O despite|O this|O high|O mortality|O ,|O McCormick|O and|O Gagliano|O (|O in|O press|O [36]|O )|O showed|O that|O for|O P|O .|O amboinensis|O there|O is|O a|O relationship|O between|O the|O size|O of|O the|O otolith|O at|O hatching|O and|O who|O changes|O sex|O to|O become|O the|O dominant|O male|O later|O in|O life|O ;|O that|O is|O ,|O early|O life|O history|O somehow|O pro|O -|O rates|O subsequent|O individual|O success|O .|O
